        function sfsi_processfurther(ref) {
            var feed_id = 'QkQ4UEtXMzdUb0xBYWpBRXJ6TDE1RHpjakZ4VFZ2TG8vWGg5d1VkSllkLzYwdHVJZUVKdzYxRTNtcnQ1U0VuTEkrSHhnU3NBZHpGQnB1bXNwZzJYOGt5OWlaR0ZYU1U1dE5HOXJOZXNUbWh0S3BITU5OQUNuRmhGTWErMEtUOTh8ZGNKK2ZIUTRTajd1UEo0bFQxcEQ4OFAvZWNYbXhWYVlnVHRTd2xCTDc1cz0=';

            if ((email != "Enter your email") && (filter.test(email))) {
                if (feedtype == "8") {

                }

                alert("Please enter email address");
                jQuery(ref).find('input[name="email"]').focus();

            }
